| **Documents Required** | • Duly filled and signed PMJJBY Enrollment Form (Mandate/Consent Form). • Proof of identity and address (Aadhaar Card, PAN Card, or other KYC documents, if required by the bank). • Savings Bank Accoun |
| **Application Process** | 1. Identify Bank/Account: Ensure you possess an individual Savings Bank Account with a bank that has tied up with an authorized insurance company for PMJJBY. 2. Obtain Enrollment Form: Secure the Enro |
| **Exclusions** | • Coverage ceases automatically once the insured member attains the age of 55 years (no further renewal is permitted). • The policy is terminated if the bank account linked for premium debit is closed |

| **Exclusions** | • Households residing in urban municipal areas (The Act is strictly limited to rural areas). • Individuals under the age of 18 years. • Work demanding specialized skills or technical knowledge (The Ac |

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **ID** | 14 |

## 42. Scholarships for Students with Disabilities

| Field | Value |
|---|---|
| **ID** | 42 |
| **Category** | Education |
| **Description** | Pre-matric, Post-matric, and Top Class Education scholarships. |
| **Eligibility** | • Must be a student. • Pursuing Class 11th to Master's Degree. • Disability percentage 40% or above. • Family income < ₹2.5 Lakh/year. |
| **Benefits** | • Maintenance Allowance: ₹1600/month (Hostellers), ₹750/month (Day Scholars) • Book Allowance: ₹1500/year • Disability Allowance: ₹2000-4000/year |
| **Documents Required** | • Photograph • Proof of Age • Disability Certificate • Income Certificate • Tuition Fee Receipt. |
| **Application Process** | 1. Register at scholarships.gov.in 2. Fill application form with ID and password. 3. Upload documents. 4. Final Submit. |
| **Exclusions** | • Not for more than two students from a family. • Cannot hold any other scholarship. • False info leads to recovery with 15% interest. • No scholarship for repeat year. |
| **Portal Link** | — |
| **State(s)** | — |
| **Age Range** | — – — yrs |
| **Max Income** | ₹250000 |
| **Gender** | Male, Female, Transgender |
| **Caste** | — |
| **Occupation** | Student |
| **Ration Card** | — |
| **Disability Required** | Yes |
| **Residence** | Any |
| **Minority** | Any |
| **Senior Citizen** | Any |
| **Widow/Single Woman** | Any |
| **Tribal** | — |
| **Orphan** | — |
| **Aadhaar Required** | — |
| **Bank Account Required** | — |
| **Min Education** | — |

| Field | Value |

| **ID** | 58 |
| **Category** | Education |
| **Description** | A comprehensive scholarship scheme for students with disabilities pursuing higher education. |
| **Eligibility** | • Must be a student. • Pursuing Class 11th to Master's Degree. • Disability percentage 40% or above. • Family income < ₹2.5 Lakh/year. |
| **Benefits** | • Maintenance Allowance: ₹1600/month (Hostellers), ₹750/month (Day Scholars) • Book Allowance: ₹1500/year • Disability Allowance: ₹2000-4000/year |
| **Documents Required** | • Photograph • Proof of Age • Disability Certificate • Income Certificate • Tuition Fee Receipt. |
| **Application Process** | 1. Register at scholarships.gov.in 2. Fill application form with ID and password. 3. Upload documents. 4. Final Submit. |
| **Exclusions** | • Not for more than two students from a family. • Cannot hold any other scholarship. • False info leads to recovery with 15% interest. • No scholarship for repeat year. |
